</svg></div></a></div><div id="mobile-menu-cta" class="navbarv2-mobile-cta-wrapper"><a id="fixed-primary" href="/pricing" class="synthesia-button is-stretched w-inline-block"><div>Get started</div></a><a button="book-a-demo" href="#" class="synthesia-button-secondary is-stretched w-inline-block"><div>Book a demo</div></a></div></div><div class="navbarv2_background-overlay"></div></div></div></div></div></nav><div class="navbar-custom-scripts w-embed w-script"><script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const NAVBAR_HIDE_SCROLL_DELTA = 40; // Scroll delta to hide navbar
    const NAVBAR_SHOW_SCROLL_DELTA = -20; // Scroll delta to show navbar
    const VARIANT_CHANGE_SCROLL_THRESHOLD = 80; // Scroll threshold for changing the navbar variant
    const RESPONSIVE_WIDTH_QUERY = '(max-width: 767px)'; // Media query for responsive behavior
    const THROTTLE_DELAY = 30; // Delay in ms for the throttle function

    const navbar = document.getElementById('nav'); // Select navbar
    const stickySections = document.querySelectorAll('[data-sticky-section]'); // Select sticky sections
    const originalVariant = navbar.getAttribute('variant'); // Store the original value
    let lastScrollPosition = 0; // Track of the last scroll position
    let cumulativeScrollDelta = 0; // Track cumulative scroll distance
    let isAnchorLink = window.location.hash; // Check if URL contains an anchor link
    let initialLoad = true; // Flag to track initial load

    // Function to check and update the navbar variant on load
    function checkAndUpdateNavbarVariantOnLoad() {
        let initialScrollPosition = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
        if (initialScrollPosition > VARIANT_CHANGE_SCROLL_THRESHOLD) {
            navbar.setAttribute('variant', 'null');
        } else {
            navbar.setAttribute('variant', originalVariant);
        }
    }

    // Function to update sticky sections based on navbar visibility
    function updateStickySections(hidden) {
        stickySections.forEach(section => {
            if (hidden) {
                section.classList.add('navbar-hidden-sticky');
            } else {
                section.classList.remove('navbar-hidden-sticky');
            }
        });
    }

    // Function to handle scroll events
    function handleScroll() {
        let currentScrollPosition = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
        let scrollDelta = currentScrollPosition - lastScrollPosition;

        if ((cumulativeScrollDelta > 0 && scrollDelta < 0) || (cumulativeScrollDelta < 0 && scrollDelta > 0)) {
            cumulativeScrollDelta = scrollDelta;
        } else {
            cumulativeScrollDelta += scrollDelta;
        }

        // Apply style changes only if screen width is below threshold
        if (window.matchMedia(RESPONSIVE_WIDTH_QUERY).matches) {
            if (!initialLoad || !isAnchorLink) {
                applyNavbarStyleChanges();
            }
        }

        // After first scroll, set initialLoad to false
        initialLoad = false;

        // Update the last scroll position
        lastScrollPosition = currentScrollPosition;

        // Check scroll position for variant attribute change
        if (currentScrollPosition > VARIANT_CHANGE_SCROLL_THRESHOLD) {
            navbar.setAttribute('variant', 'null');
        } else {
            navbar.setAttribute('variant', originalVariant);
        }
    }

    // Function to apply style changes to the navbar
    function applyNavbarStyleChanges() {
        if (cumulativeScrollDelta > NAVBAR_HIDE_SCROLL_DELTA && window.scrollY > 50) {
            navbar.classList.add('navbar-hidden'); // Update navbar position
            updateStickySections(true); // Update sticky position
            cumulativeScrollDelta = 0; // Reset cumulative scroll
        } else if (cumulativeScrollDelta < NAVBAR_SHOW_SCROLL_DELTA) {
            navbar.classList.remove('navbar-hidden'); // Update navbar position
            updateStickySections(false); // Update sticky position
            cumulativeScrollDelta = 0; // Reset cumulative scroll
        }
    }

    // Throttle function to limit the rate of function execution
    function throttle(func, limit) {
        let lastFunc;
        let lastRan;
        return function() {
            const context = this;
            const args = arguments;
            if (!lastRan) {
                func.apply(context, args);
                lastRan = Date.now();
            } else {
                clearTimeout(lastFunc);
                lastFunc = setTimeout(function() {
                    if ((Date.now() - lastRan) >= limit) {
                        func.apply(context, args);
                        lastRan = Date.now();
                    }
                }, limit - (Date.now() - lastRan));
            }
        };
    }

    // Call function to check and update navbar variant on initial load
    checkAndUpdateNavbarVariantOnLoad();

    // Add scroll event listener with throttled handler
    window.addEventListener('scroll', throttle(handleScroll, THROTTLE_DELAY));
});


/* START - NO SCROLL WHEN MOBILE MENU IS OPEN + COMBO CLASS FOR TRANSPARENT STYLING */
// Set overflow:hidden on body when clicking burger menu
document.querySelector('.navbarv2_burger-menu-wrapper').addEventListener('click', function() {
    var element = this;
    var clicks = element.getAttribute('data-clicks') === 'true'; // because data attributes return as string

    if (clicks) {
        document.body.style.overflow = 'auto';
        document.querySelector('#nav').classList.remove('opened')
    } else {
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
        document.querySelector('#nav').classList.add('opened')
    }

    element.setAttribute('data-clicks', !clicks);
});

// Enable scroll on anchor link click
navLinkItems = document.querySelectorAll('.navbarv2_menu-list-wrapper a');

for (let navLink of navLinkItems) {
    navLink.addEventListener('click', function() {
        document.querySelector('body').style.overflow = 'auto';
        document.querySelector('#nav').classList.remove('opened');
    });
}
/* END - NO SCROLL WHEN MOBILE MENU IS OPEN + COMBO CLASS FOR TRANSPARENT STYLING */


/* START - NAVLINK BOLD ON HOVER */
// Automatically assign an attribute to each navbar link with same value as the link-text
let navTopLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.navbarv2_link')
for (let topLink of navTopLinks) {
    topLink.setAttribute('title', `${topLink.innerText}`)
}
/* END - NAVLINK BOLD ON HOVER */
</script></div></div><div class="page-wrapper"><div class="transparent-navbar_spacer"></div><header data-w-id="71bdb6b2-00fb-a90e-86d3-0e8c0e0db5f0" class="section_career-hero"><div class="z-2"><div class="page-padding"><div class="container-large"><div class="w-layout-grid header76_component"><div id="w-node-_71bdb6b2-00fb-a90e-86d3-0e8c0e0db5f5-0e0db5f0" class="header76_content-left"><a href="https://www.g2.com/best-software-companies/2024/fastest-growing" target="_blank" class="badge-flag is-small is-synthesia-blue is-cursor-pointer w-inline-block"><div class="icon-flag w-embed"><svg width="16" height="18" viewBox="0 0 16 18" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">

/* Display job posts career page */

function fetchPositions() {
    fetch("https://boards-api.greenhouse.io/v1/boards/synthesia/departments")
        .then((response) => response.json())
        .then((data) => {
            console.log("API Data:", data);
            processData(data);
            populateFilters(data);
            filterJobs();
        })
        .catch((error) => console.error("Error fetching data:", error))
        .finally(() => {
            setTimeout(() => {
                const careerComponent = document.querySelector(".career2_component");
                adjustAccordionBorder(careerComponent);
                careerComponent.style.opacity = 1;

                if (window.innerWidth < 767) {
                    const accordions = document.querySelectorAll(".career2_accordion");
                    for (let i = 1; i < accordions.length; i++) {
                        const list = accordions[i].querySelector('.career2_list');
                        list.style.display = "none";
                        const iconWrapper = accordions[i].querySelector('.career2_icon-wrapper');
                        iconWrapper.classList.add("rotate");
                    }
                }
            }, 0);
        });
}

function adjustAccordionBorder(element) {
    const careerAccordion = element.querySelector(".career2_accordion");
    if (element.children.length === 1) {
        if (careerAccordion) {
            careerAccordion.style.borderBottom = "none";
        }
    } else if (element.children.length > 1) {
        if (careerAccordion) {
            careerAccordion.style.borderBottom = "1px solid var(--grey-medium)";
        }
    }
}

function processData(data) {
    const careerComponent = document.querySelector(".career2_component");
    const jobDepartment = document.querySelector(".career2_job-department");
    const jobItem = document.querySelector(".career2_item");
    careerComponent.innerHTML = "";
    data.departments.forEach((department) => {
        if (department.jobs.length > 0) {
            const departmentNode = jobDepartment.cloneNode(true);
            departmentNode.querySelector('[identifier="job-department-title"]').textContent = department.name;
            departmentNode.addEventListener("click", () => toggleList(departmentNode.nextElementSibling));
            const accordion = document.createElement("div");
            accordion.classList.add("career2_accordion");
            accordion.id = `accordion-${department.name}`;
            accordion.appendChild(departmentNode);
            const list = document.createElement("div");
            list.classList.add("career2_list");
            list.id = `${department.name.toLowerCase()}-list`;
            accordion.appendChild(list);
            department.jobs.forEach((job) => {
                const jobNode = jobItem.cloneNode(true);
                jobNode.querySelector('[identifier="job-title"]').textContent = job.title;
                jobNode.querySelector('[identifier="job-location"]').textContent = job.location.name;
                jobNode.querySelector('[identifier="job-link"]').setAttribute("href", job.absolute_url);
                list.appendChild(jobNode);
            });
            careerComponent.appendChild(accordion);
        }
    });
}

function populateFilters(data) {
    const departmentSelect = document.querySelector('[identifier="department-select"]');
    const officeSelect = document.querySelector('[identifier="office-select"]');
    const clearDepartment = document.querySelector('[identifier="clear-department"]');
    const clearOffice = document.querySelector('[identifier="clear-office"]');
    clearDepartment.addEventListener("click", () => {
        departmentSelect.value = "";
        filterJobs();
    });
    clearOffice.addEventListener("click", () => {
        officeSelect.value = "";
        filterJobs();
    });
    data.departments.forEach((department) => {
        if (department.jobs.length > 0) {
            const departmentOption = document.createElement("option");
            departmentOption.value = department.name;
            departmentOption.text = department.name;
            departmentSelect.appendChild(departmentOption);
            department.jobs.forEach((job) => {
                const location = job.location.name;
                const officeOption = document.createElement("option");
                officeOption.value = location;
                officeOption.text = location;
                if (!officeSelect.innerHTML.includes(officeOption.outerHTML)) {
                    officeSelect.appendChild(officeOption);
                }
            });
        }
    });
    departmentSelect.addEventListener("change", () => filterJobs());
    officeSelect.addEventListener("change", () => filterJobs());
}

function filterJobs() {
    const careerComponent = document.querySelector(".career2_component");
    adjustAccordionBorder(careerComponent);
    const departmentSelect = document.querySelector('[identifier="department-select"]');
    const officeSelect = document.querySelector('[identifier="office-select"]');
    const accordions = document.querySelectorAll(".career2_accordion");
    let foundJobs = false;
    accordions.forEach((accordion) => {
        const jobItems = accordion.querySelectorAll(".career2_list .career2_item");
        const departmentTitle = accordion.querySelector('[identifier="job-department-title"]').textContent.trim().toLowerCase();
        let found = false;
        jobItems.forEach((item) => {
            item.querySelector('[identifier="job-title"]').textContent.toLowerCase();
            const jobLocation = item.querySelector('[identifier="job-location"]').textContent.toLowerCase();
            const selectedDepartment = departmentSelect.value.toLowerCase();
            const selectedOffice = officeSelect.value.toLowerCase();
            if ((selectedDepartment !== "") && (!departmentTitle.includes(selectedDepartment)) || (selectedOffice !== "") && (!jobLocation.includes(selectedOffice))) {
                item.style.display = "none";
            } else {
                item.style.display = "block";
                found = true;
                foundJobs = true;
            }
        });
        if (found) {
            accordion.style.display = "block";
            accordion.querySelector(".career2_list").style.display = "block";
        } else {
            accordion.style.display = "none";
        }
    });
    
}

function toggleList(element) {
    const display = getComputedStyle(element).display !== "none";
    element.style.display = display ? "none" : "block";
    element.previousElementSibling.querySelector(".career2_icon-wrapper").classList.toggle("rotate");
}

window.onload = fetchPositions;



</script></div></div></div></div></section><section class="section_career-news"><div class="divider"></div><div id="live-webinars" class="anchor-point"></div><div class="page-padding"><div class="container-large"><div class="padding-vertical padding-xhuge"><div><div class="margin-bottom margin-xlarge"><div class="margin-bottom margin-small-2-2"><div class="margin-bottom margin-xsmall-2-2"><div class="caption-1 text-color-synthesia-blue-primary">PRESS</div></div><h2 class="heading-style-h1 archia">Synthesia in the news<br/></h2></div></div></div><div class="w-embed"><style>
.example-item.fade-out{
	opacity: 0.4;
		transition: 0.6s ease;
}
.example-item{
	opacity: 1;
	transition: 0.6s ease;
}
.example_recoomended-item.w-dyn-item a {

  // Function to Retrieve Cookie Value
  function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
    const name = `${cookieName}=`;
    const decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
    const cookies = decodedCookie.split(';').map(cookie => cookie.trim());
    return cookies.find(cookie => cookie.startsWith(name))?.substring(name.length) || "";
  }

  // Set Facebook Pixel and LinkedIn Insight Tag values
  const fbpValue = getCookieValue("_fbp");
  if (fbpValue) document.querySelector("#fbp").value = fbpValue;

  const fbcValue = getCookieValue('_fbc');
  if (fbcValue) document.querySelector('#fbc').value = fbcValue;

  const liClid = getCookieValue('li_fat_id');
  if (liClid) document.querySelector('#liclid').value = liClid;

    function getCookie(name) {
    let cookieArr = document.cookie.split(";");
    for(let i = 0; i < cookieArr.length; i++) {
        let cookiePair = cookieArr[i].split("=");
        if(name == cookiePair[0].trim()) {
            return decodeURIComponent(cookiePair[1]);
        }
    }
    return null;
}

function setClientIdInHiddenField() {
    let gaCookie = getCookie("_ga");
    if (gaCookie) {
        // The Client ID is after the second dot in the _ga cookie
        let clientId = gaCookie.split('.').slice(2).join(".");
        //console.log(clientId)
        let hiddenField = document.querySelector('#ga_client_id');
        if (hiddenField) {
            hiddenField.value = clientId;
        }
    }
}

setClientIdInHiddenField();

function GAgetSessionData() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        const pattern = /_ga_ETJWNCCEC5=GS\d\.\d\.(.+?)(?:;|$)/;

        const tryExtractData = () => {
            const match = document.cookie.match(pattern);
            const parts = match?.[1].split(".");

            if (!parts) {
                // Cookie not yet available; wait a bit and try again.
                setTimeout(tryExtractData, 200);
            } else {
                resolve({
                    ga_session_id: parts.shift(),
                    ga_session_number: parts.shift(),
                });
            }
        };

        tryExtractData();
    });
}

GAgetSessionData().then(sessionData => {
	document.querySelector('#ga_session_id').value = sessionData.ga_session_id; 
    //console.log("GA Session ID:", sessionData.ga_session_id);
    //console.log("GA Session Number:", sessionData.ga_session_number);
    // Further processing with sessionData
}).catch(error => {
    console.error("Error getting session data:", error);
});

function validateEmail(email) {
  const regex =
    /^^([\w-\.]+@(?!gmail)(?!yahoo)(?!hotmail)(?!aol.com)(?!abc.com)(?!xyz.com)(?!pqr.com)(?!rediffmail.com)(?!live.com)(?!outlook)(?!me.com)(?!msn.com)(?!ymail.com)(?!mail.ru)(?!protonmail)(?!icloud)(?!yopmail)(?!gmial)(?!gamil)(?!hostvn.net)(?!email.com)(?!vodamail)(?!yandex)([\w-]+\.)+[\w-]{2,10})?$/;
  return regex.test(email);
}

function validatePhone() {
  const phoneValue = phoneField.value.trim();
  const isPhoneValid =
    phoneValue.length >= 6 && phoneValue.length <= 17 && /^[\d-+\s()]+$/.test(phoneValue);
  phoneField.value = phoneValue.replace(/[^0-9+\-()\s]/g, ""); // Remove invalid characters

  // Log to the console based on the validity of the phone number
  if (!isPhoneValid) {
      phoneError.style.display = "block";
  } 
  else {
      phoneError.style.display = "none";
  }
  if(phoneField.dataset.userInteracted === "false"){
      phoneError.style.display = "none";
  }

  return isPhoneValid;
}

/*
function isRecaptchaCompleted() {

}

function validateStepOne() {
  const stepOneFieldsValid = Array.from(requiredFieldsStepOne).every(
    (field) => {
      if (field.type === "email") {
        return validateEmail(field.value);
      } else if (field === phoneField) {
        return validatePhone();
      } else {
        return field.value.trim() !== "";
      }
    }
  );

  nextButton.classList.toggle("is-disabled", !stepOneFieldsValid);
}

function validateForm() {
  const allFieldsValid =
    Array.from(requiredFields).every((field) => {
      if (field.type === "email") {
        return validateEmail(field.value);
      } else {
        return field.value.trim() !== "";
      }
    }) &&
    guidelinesCheckbox.checked;
//    guidelinesCheckbox.checked &&
//    isRecaptchaCompleted();

  submitButton.classList.toggle("is-disabled", !allFieldsValid);
}

demoForm.addEventListener("input", validateForm);
requiredFieldsStepOne.forEach((field) =>
  field.addEventListener("input", validateStepOne)
);

emailField.addEventListener("blur", () => {
  if (!validateEmail(emailField.value)) {
    emailError.classList.add("expose");
  } else {
    emailError.classList.remove("expose");

phoneField.dataset.userInteracted = "false";

  phoneField.dataset.userInteracted = "true";

  validateStepOne();

// Resize fix
var optimizedResize = debounce(function () {
  Webflow.ready();
}, 1000);

window.addEventListener("resize", optimizedResize);

function debounce(func, wait, immediate) {
  var timeout;
  return function () {
    var context = this,
      args = arguments;
    var later = function () {
      timeout = null;
      if (!immediate) func.apply(context, args);
    };
    var callNow = immediate && !timeout;
    clearTimeout(timeout);
    timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
    if (callNow) func.apply(context, args);
  };
}



// Define the function
function handleEscapeKey(event) {
if (event.key === 'Escape') {
  console.log('escape');
   demoFormModal.style.display = "none";
  document.querySelector("html").style.overflow = "auto";
  removeEscapeKeyListener()
}
}
  function removeEscapeKeyListener() {
      document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleEscapeKey);
}



for (var i = 0; i < requiredFieldsStepOne.length; i++) {
  requiredFieldsStepOne[i].addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
    if (event.which == "13") {
      event.preventDefault();
      if (!nextButton.classList.contains("is-disabled")) {
        nextButton.click();
      }
      return;
    }
  });
}

// Check iv user comes via Product
function checkQueryParam() {
  // Create a URLSearchParams instance with the current query string
  const params = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

  // Check if 'bookADemo' parameter is present and set to 'true'
  if (params.get('bookADemo') === 'true') {
	document.querySelector('input[name="product_traffic"]').value = 'true'
  }
}

// Call the function to check the URL
checkQueryParam();

<script>
  Webflow.push(function () {
    // Center on active item for horizontal scroll elements.
    $(".w-tab-menu a").on("click", function () {
      jQuery(".w-tab-menu a").removeClass("active");
      jQuery(this).addClass("active");
      // CALL scrollCenter PLUSGIN
      jQuery(".w-tab-menu").scrollCenter(".active", 300);
    });

    jQuery.fn.scrollCenter = function (elem, speed) {
      var active = jQuery(this).find(elem); // find the active element
      var activeWidth = active.width() / 2; // get active width center
      var pos = active.position().left + activeWidth; //get left position of active li + center position
      var elpos = jQuery(this).scrollLeft(); // get current scroll position
      var elW = jQuery(this).width(); //get div width
      pos = pos + elpos - elW / 2; // for center position if you want adjust then change this
      jQuery(this).animate(
        {
          scrollLeft: pos,
        },
        speed == undefined ? 1000 : speed
      );
      return this;
    };
    jQuery.fn.scrollCenterORI = function (elem, speed) {
      jQuery(this).animate(
        {
          scrollLeft:
            jQuery(this).scrollLeft() -
            jQuery(this).offset().left +
            jQuery(elem).offset().left,
        },
        speed == undefined ? 1000 : speed
      );
      return this;
    };
  });
</script>

<script>
  // Sent body to overflow hidden on first click of hamburger icon
  $(".menu-parent").click(function () {
    var clicks = $(this).data("clicks");
    if (clicks) {
      $("body").css("overflow", "auto");
    } else {
      $("body").css("overflow", "hidden");
    }
    $(this).data("clicks", !clicks);
  });
</script>

<!-- Lazy load HTML videos -->
<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    var lazyVideos = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll("video.lazy"));

    if ("IntersectionObserver" in window) {
      var lazyVideoObserver = new IntersectionObserver(function (
        entries,
        observer
      ) {
        entries.forEach(function (video) {
          if (video.isIntersecting) {
            for (var source in video.target.children) {
              var videoSource = video.target.children[source];
              if (
                typeof videoSource.tagName === "string" &&
                videoSource.tagName === "SOURCE"
              ) {
                videoSource.src = videoSource.dataset.src;
              }
            }

            video.target.load();
            video.target.classList.remove("lazy");
            lazyVideoObserver.unobserve(video.target);
          }
        });
      });

      lazyVideos.forEach(function (lazyVideo) {
        lazyVideoObserver.observe(lazyVideo);
      });
    }
  });
</script>

<!-- Custom Recaptcha loaded when form has recaptcha -->

<style>
  .gresponse-await{
  opacity: 0.2;
  pointer-events: none;
  user-seclect: none;
  }
</style>
<!-- Custom Recaptcha loaded when form has recaptcha -->
<script>
window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
    const forms = document.querySelectorAll("form");
  
    forms.forEach((form) => {
      const recaptchaElement = form.querySelector(".g-recaptcha");
      if (recaptchaElement) {
        const formParent = form.closest(".form-modal");
        const submitButton = form.querySelector('input[type="submit"]');
        // Initially hide the submit button
  
        // Assuming 'form' is already defined and refers to your form element
  
        // Check if the element has the attribute and if it equals "recaptchaCallback"
        if (
          recaptchaElement &&
          recaptchaElement.getAttribute("data-callback") === "recaptchaCallback"
        ) {
          setTimeout(() => {
  submitButton.classList.add("gresponse-await");
  submitButton.setAttribute('disabled', '');
}, 0);
         // console.log(submitButton);
  
        } else {
         
        }
  
        if (formParent) {
          const observer = new MutationObserver((mutationsList) => {
            mutationsList.forEach((mutation) => {
              if (
                mutation.type === "attributes" &&
                mutation.attributeName === "class"
              ) {
                console.log("Class attribute changed in .form-modal");
                if (formParent.classList.contains("open-modal")) {
                  console.log("Open-modal class added to .form-modal");
                  recaptchaCallback(recaptchaElement, form, submitButton);
                  observer.disconnect();
                }
              }
            });
          });
  
          observer.observe(formParent, { attributes: true });
        } else {
          const formObserver = new IntersectionObserver(
            (entries) => {
              entries.forEach((entry) => {
                if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                  console.log("Form is visible");
                  recaptchaCallback(recaptchaElement, form, submitButton);
                  formObserver.disconnect();
                }
              });
            },
            { threshold: 0.1 }
          );
  
          formObserver.observe(form);
        }
      }
    });
  
    function recaptchaCallback(recaptchaElement, form, submitButton) {
      console.log("Executing reCAPTCHA function");
      recaptchaElement.setAttribute(
        "data-sitekey",
        "6LeTwvUiAAAAAPvqL8BzAIeHJuvvhijJZcxYMo4A"
      );
      const recaptchaScript = document.createElement("script");
      recaptchaScript.src = "https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js";
      document.body.appendChild(recaptchaScript);
  
      window.recaptchaCallback = function () {
        console.log("reCAPTCHA verification successful");
        // Remove the .invisible class from the submit button
        submitButton.classList.remove("gresponse-await");
        submitButton.removeAttribute('disabled');
        // Your logic to handle successful reCAPTCHA verification and form submission
        form.addEventListener("submit", handleSubmit);
      };
    }
  
    function handleSubmit(event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      const recaptchaResponse = document.querySelector("#g-recaptcha-response");
      if (recaptchaResponse.value === "") {
        displayErrorMessage("Please validate Recaptcha", recaptchaResponse);
      } else {
        // Your logic to handle the form submission (e.g., AJAX request, form submit, etc.)
        console.log("Form submitted successfully!");
        // Uncomment the line below to submit the form:
        // event.target.submit();
      }
    }
  
    function displayErrorMessage(message, element) {
      const errorMessage = document.createElement("span");
      errorMessage.classList.add("error-message");
      errorMessage.textContent = message;
      element.parentNode.appendChild(errorMessage);
    }
  });

</script>
<!-- END Recaptcha loaded when form has recaptcha -->

<!-- Start - Capture gclid in forms -->
<script>
// Step 1: Capture GCLID on page load and store in session storage
function captureGCLID() {
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const gclid = urlParams.get('gclid');
    if (gclid) {
        // Store GCLID in session storage
        sessionStorage.setItem('gclid', gclid);
        console.log("GCLID found and stored in session storage:", gclid);
    }
}

// Ensure the function runs when the document is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', captureGCLID);



// Step 2: Update the forms hidden field with GCLID
function setGclidField() {
	 const gclidField = document.querySelector('#gclid');
	 if(gclidField){
	 	  const gclid = sessionStorage.getItem('gclid');
	 	  if(gclid){
	 	  	 gclidField.value = gclid;
	 	  }
	 }
}

// Ensure the function runs when the document is loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', setGclidField);
</script>
<!-- End - Capture gclid in forms --></body></html>
